is a measure of:

b) Morbidity only

Disability).]

 35. Polio has been absent in India since
     2014. Routine surveillance
     continues for AFP (Acute Flaccid
     Paralysis) cases. Which term
     correctly describes the current
     status of polio in India?
      a) Eradicated                          Disability → Handicap
      b) Eliminated
      c) Controlled



d) Extinct

ANSWER: b). Eliminated

[Elimination = zero incidence in a
defined geographical area, but the
agent still exists elsewhere; Eradication
= complete and permanent worldwide
reduction to zero cases]

the correct chronological sequence

     epidemic is:                                  negatives = 10
     a) Influenza                              ▪ Sensitivity = (90 / (90+10)) × 100
     b) Food poisoning                             = 90%

     d) COVID-19                               has sensitivity of 95% and

  ANSWER: b)                                   prevalence is 10%, what is the
  136. In a village of 1000 people, 100
     people were found to have
     tuberculosis (TB). During one year,
     20 new cases were detected. What
     is the incidence rate of TB in this
     village?                                     d) 51.3%
      a) 1%                                 ANSWER: c). 52.7%
      b) 2%
      c) 10%                                        Explanation:
      d) 20%                                   ▪ Diseased = 10% of 1000 = 100

  ANSWER: a). 2%                                    Test results:
     ▪    Explanation:                         ▪ True Positives = 95% of 100 = 95
     ▪    Incidence rate = (New cases
          during a period / Population at
          risk) × 100                               810
      ▪ Here, new cases = 20
      ▪ Population at risk = Total
          population – Prevalent cases =
          1000 – 100 = 900
      ▪ So, incidence rate = (20 / 900) ×
          100 = 2.22% ≈ 2%

b) 90%
c) 91%

▪   Explanation:

       the Interview, Patient's Perception,
       Invitation, Knowledge, Emotions with
       Empathic Responses, and Strategy
       and Summary, a framework for
       delivering bad news.
